GreatGame_Category = {
	GreatGame_game_1_turn_1_mission = {
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = { always = no }
		icon = GFX_decision_chess_king
		priority = 10

		days_mission_timeout = 60
		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GreatGame_game_1_turn_1_mission"
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout GreatGame_game_1_turn_1_mission"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = GER }
				add_to_array = { global.great_game_array = 1 }
				great_game_end_turn = yes
				great_game_var_setup = yes
				set_variable = { global.great_game_turn = 2 }
				hidden_effect = {
					activate_mission = GreatGame_game_1_turn_2_mission
					ITA = { activate_mission = GreatGame_game_1_turn_2_mission }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	GreatGame_GER_game_1_turn_1_decision_1 = {
		icon = GFX_decision_SAF_buy_pakt_guns
		visible = {
			has_active_mission = GreatGame_game_1_turn_1_mission
			hidden_trigger = {
				tag = GER
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
					has_country_flag = GreatGame_round_lost
				}
			}
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 1999 }
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 10
		cancel_trigger = {
			NOT = { has_active_mission = GreatGame_game_1_turn_1_mission }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					check_variable = { GER.great_game_number > ITA.great_game_number }
					check_variable = { ITA.great_game_number > 9 }
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GreatGame_GER_game_1_turn_1_decision_1"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = GER }
				hidden_effect = {
					ITA = { activate_decision = GreatGame_GER_game_1_turn_1_decision_1 }
				}
				set_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -2000
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove GreatGame_GER_game_1_turn_1_decision_1"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = GER }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_low = 2 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_high = 4 }
				great_game_add_points = yes
				great_game_round_loss_check = yes
				clr_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = great_game_GER_decision_tt
			}
		}
	}
	GreatGame_ITA_game_1_turn_1_decision_1 = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse
		visible = {
			has_active_mission = GreatGame_game_1_turn_1_mission
			hidden_trigger = {
				tag = ITA
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken

		fire_only_once = yes

		cancel_trigger = {
			NOT = { has_active_mission = GreatGame_game_1_turn_1_mission }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					check_variable = { ITA.great_game_number > GER.great_game_number }
					check_variable = { GER.great_game_number > 9 }
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GreatGame_ITA_game_1_turn_1_decision_1"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = ITA }
				hidden_effect = {
					GER = { activate_decision = GreatGame_ITA_game_1_turn_1_decision_1 }
				}
				set_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
				add_political_power = -25
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove GreatGame_ITA_game_1_turn_1_decision_1"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = ITA }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_low = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_high = 4 }
				great_game_add_points = yes
				great_game_round_loss_check = yes
				clr_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = great_game_ITA_decision_tt
			}
		}
	}

				clr_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = great_game_ITA_decision_tt
			}
		}
	}
	GreatGame_GER_game_3_turn_5_decision_6 = {
		icon = GFX_decision_SAF_buy_pakt_guns
		visible = {
			has_active_mission = GreatGame_game_3_turn_5_mission
			hidden_trigger = {
				tag = GER
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
					has_country_flag = GreatGame_round_lost
				}
			}
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 999 }
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 10
		cancel_trigger = {
			NOT = { has_active_mission = GreatGame_game_3_turn_5_mission }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					check_variable = { GER.great_game_number > ITA.great_game_number }
					check_variable = { ITA.great_game_number > 9 }
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GreatGame_GER_game_3_turn_5_decision_6"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = GER }
				hidden_effect = {
					ITA = { activate_decision = GreatGame_GER_game_3_turn_5_decision_6 }
				}
				set_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -1000
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove GreatGame_GER_game_3_turn_5_decision_6"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = GER }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_low = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_high = 3 }
				great_game_add_points = yes
				great_game_round_loss_check = yes
				clr_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = great_game_GER_decision_tt
			}
		}
	}

	GreatGame_game_5_turn_1_mission = {
		icon = GFX_decision_chess_king
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = { always = no }

		priority = 10

		days_mission_timeout = 60
		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GreatGame_game_5_turn_1_mission"
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout GreatGame_game_5_turn_1_mission"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = GER }
				add_to_array = { global.great_game_array = 1 }
				great_game_end_turn = yes
				great_game_var_setup = yes
				set_variable = { global.great_game_turn = 2 }
				hidden_effect = {
					activate_mission = GreatGame_game_5_turn_2_mission
					ITA = { activate_mission = GreatGame_game_5_turn_2_mission }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	GreatGame_GER_game_5_turn_1_decision_1 = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_parade
		visible = {
			has_active_mission = GreatGame_game_5_turn_1_mission
			hidden_trigger = {
				tag = GER
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
					has_country_flag = GreatGame_round_lost
				}
			}
			has_manpower > 4999
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 10
		cancel_trigger = {
			NOT = { has_active_mission = GreatGame_game_5_turn_1_mission }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					check_variable = { GER.great_game_number > ITA.great_game_number }
					check_variable = { ITA.great_game_number > 9 }
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GreatGame_GER_game_5_turn_1_decision_1"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = GER }
				hidden_effect = {
					ITA = { activate_decision = GreatGame_GER_game_5_turn_1_decision_1 }
				}
				set_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
				add_manpower = -5000
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove GreatGame_GER_game_5_turn_1_decision_1"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = GER }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_low = 2 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_high = 4 }
				great_game_add_points = yes
				great_game_round_loss_check = yes
				clr_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = great_game_GER_decision_tt
			}
		}
	}
	GreatGame_ITA_game_5_turn_1_decision_1 = {
		icon = GFX_decision_humanitarian_aid_increase
		visible = {
			has_active_mission = GreatGame_game_5_turn_1_mission
			hidden_trigger = {
				tag = ITA
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
					has_country_flag = GreatGame_round_lost
				}
			}
			has_equipment = { support_equipment > 499 }
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 10
		cancel_trigger = {
			NOT = { has_active_mission = GreatGame_game_5_turn_1_mission }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					check_variable = { ITA.great_game_number > GER.great_game_number }
					check_variable = { GER.great_game_number > 9 }
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GreatGame_ITA_game_5_turn_1_decision_1"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = ITA }
				hidden_effect = {
					GER = { activate_decision = GreatGame_ITA_game_5_turn_1_decision_1 }
				}
				set_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = -500
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove GreatGame_ITA_game_5_turn_1_decision_1"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = ITA }
				SER = {
					TNO_improve_poverty_low = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { temp_low = 2 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_high = 4 }
				great_game_add_points = yes
				great_game_round_loss_check = yes
				clr_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = great_game_ITA_decision_tt
			}
		}
	}

	GreatGame_GER_game_5_turn_2_decision_1 = {
		icon = GFX_decision_point
		visible = {
			has_active_mission = GreatGame_game_5_turn_2_mission
			hidden_trigger = {
				tag = GER
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
					has_country_flag = GreatGame_round_lost
				}
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 10
		cancel_trigger = {
			NOT = { has_active_mission = GreatGame_game_5_turn_2_mission }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					check_variable = { GER.great_game_number > ITA.great_game_number }
					check_variable = { ITA.great_game_number > 9 }
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GreatGame_GER_game_5_turn_2_decision_1"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = GER }
				hidden_effect = {
					ITA = { activate_decision = GreatGame_GER_game_5_turn_2_decision_1 }
				}
				set_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
				set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.025 }
				econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove GreatGame_GER_game_5_turn_2_decision_1"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = GER }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_low = 2 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_high = 4 }
				great_game_add_points = yes
				great_game_round_loss_check = yes
				clr_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
				SER = {
					TNO_improve_unemployment_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = great_game_GER_decision_tt
			}
		}
	}

		icon = GFX_decision_chess_king
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = { always = no }

		priority = 10

		days_mission_timeout = 60
		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GreatGame_game_5_turn_3_mission"
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout GreatGame_game_5_turn_3_mission"
			if = {
				limit = { tag = GER }
				add_to_array = { global.great_game_array = 1 }
				great_game_end_turn = yes
				great_game_var_setup = yes
				set_variable = { global.great_game_turn = 4 }
				hidden_effect = {
					activate_mission = GreatGame_game_5_turn_4_mission
					ITA = { activate_mission = GreatGame_game_5_turn_4_mission }
				}
			}
		}
	}

			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove GreatGame_GER_game_5_turn_5_decision_4"
			if = {

				set_temp_variable = { temp_high = 3 }
				great_game_add_points = yes
				great_game_round_loss_check = yes
				clr_country_flag = GreatGame_decision_taken
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = great_game_GER_decision_tt
			}
		}
	}
